    </div>

    <div class="home__leaders-body [ row / collapsed ]">

      <!-- players -->
      <section class="home__leaders-category [ columns / large-4 ]" ng-repeat="category in players.items" ng-show="isPlayers">

        <!-- season leaders header -->
        <div class="category-header">
          <h2 class="category-header__name" ng-if="category.name=='FANTASY_POINTS'">
            <a class="category-header__fantasy-link">
              {{::category.title}}
            </a>
          </h2>

              {{::category.title}}
            </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="category-header__share" ng-if="category.name!=='FANTASY_POINTS'">

            </a>
          </div>
          <div class="clear"></div>
        </div>

                <td class="category-table__rank" ng-if="player.RANK">{{::player.RANK}}.</td>
                <td class="category-table__rank" ng-if="!player.RANK">{{::player.rank}}.</td>
                <td class="category-table__text">

                </td>

                    {{::player[category.name] | statNumber:category.permode:category.name}}
                  </a>
                </td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </section>

      <!-- teams -->
      <section class="home__leaders-category [ columns / large-4 ]" ng-repeat="category in teams.items" ng-show="isTeams">
